allowlisted	claude/CLAUDE-THEAGENCY.md	113	- **Python: 3.13+.** Framework tools, hooks, and services target modern Python. Set in D45-R1 per principal directive, superseding the D44-R6 3.12 floor. Rationale: brew default is 3.13 so adopters get the floor for free; 3.13 adds nothing we must opt into (PEP 703 no-GIL and PEP 744 JIT are opt-in). Shebang convention: `#!/usr/bin/env python3` + runtime `sys.version_info` guard (NOT `python3.13` — hard-coded minor names break pyenv/nix/conda/Apple-stock installs; see `usr/jordan/captain/briefings/python-shebang-investigation-20260418.md`). Framework tools in `claude/tools/` remain **zero-pip**: stdlib only. Services (iscp dispatch-hub, etc.) may use pip deps.

allowlisted	claude/README-THEAGENCY.md	902	A command is a slash-invoked action. rename-target	claude/REFERENCE-WORKTREE-DISCIPLINE.md	37	**Critical: never `cd` to the main checkout from a worktree.** Agent identity resolution uses the current working directory's git branch. When a worktree agent `cd`s to the main repo, `agent-identity` resolves the branch as `main` → identity becomes `captain` → handoffs and dispatches go to the wrong agent. The `cd-to-main-block` hookify rule blocks this pattern (and absolute paths to tools in the main repo). **Always use relative paths from your worktree:** `./claude/tools/dispatch list`, never `cd /path/to/main && ./claude/tools/dispatch list` or `/Users/.../the-agency/claude/tools/dispatch list`.
